[30;1m17 | [0m[35mformat variables is not dependent on what version of Python PySpelling is run on, but is based on th[0m

[30;1m19 | [0m[35m[0m

[30;1m22 | [0m[35m    `#!py3 from __future__ import unicode_literals`, it will still treat the default strings in Pyth[0m
